THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION CHEPAUK, CHENNAI-600 005.
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM C
NOTICE UNDER SECTION 3(1) OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF LAND FOR 
INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997 
(LA-I(1)/9012906/2024)
No.VI(1)/800(d-1)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be 
acquired for Industrial Purposes, to wit to Doubling of Broad-Gauge Railway Line between Eraniel and Parassala in 
Maruthoorkurichi Village of Kalkulam Taluk in Kanniyakumari District, and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by Southern 
Railways. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for 
Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring 21464 Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for Industrial Purposes to wit for the 
Doubling of Broad-Gauge Railway Line between Eraniel and Parassala in Maruthoorkurichi Village of Kalkulam Taluk 
in Kanniyakumari District.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the District Collector, Kanniyakumari District which may be inspected 
at any time during office hours.

NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION (1) OF SECTION (15) OF THE TAMIL NADU HIGHWAYS ACT, 2001
(LA- V(2)/8806424/2024)
No.VI(1)/800(d-3)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be acquired 
for Highways Department to wit for the formation of widening and improvement and formation of High level Bridge 
Kodambakkam – Sriperumbudur 13/2 and 28/8 Road, Kavanur Village in Kundrathur Taluk, Kancheepuram District and 
it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the 
funds controlled or managed by Divisional Engineer (H) (C&M), Kancheepuram, The following notice is issued under 
sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 3089 Sq.mtrs., to the 


	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
39
same, a little more or less needed for the formation of widening and improvement and formation of High level Bridge 
Kodambakkam – Sriperumbudur 13/2 and 28/8 Road in Kavanur Village, Kundrathur Taluk, Kancheepuram District.
The plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer, (LA), Highways, Kancheepuram 
and the office of the Special Tahsildar (LA), Chennai Peripheral Ring Road Project, Unit- 2, Kancheepuram may be 
inspected on any day during office hours.
